| | rgya gar skad du | buddha tsa ri ta ma hā kā bya nā ma |(p1)
bod skad du | sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po |
sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo |
dpal ldan yon tan tshogs kyis gang bdag nyid chen po sems can gyi don mdzad yang dag sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun la phyag 'tshal 
bu ram shing par mthu mnyam bu ram shing pa'i rgyud|thub dka' shākya rnams la spyod pa rnam dag pa|'phrog byed zla ba lta bur skye dgu rnams la sdug|rgyal po zas gtsang zhes bya'i ming can byung bar gyur BCt_1.1
dbang po dang mtshungs de yi bdag po ldan ma yin|nus mthu rjes mtshungs gzi brjid lha mo bde sogs dang|padmo can 'dra phun sum tshogs pa sa bzhin brtan|sgyu ma chen mo zhes bya dpe med sgyu 'dra byung BCt_1.2
mi skyong rgyal po 'di ni de dang thabs cig tu|dga' ba nyer ldan rnam thos sras kyi dpal bzhin rol|de nas yang dag ting 'dzin ldan pa'i rig ma bzhin|sdig bral ma de mngal ni rnam par bzung bar gyur BCt_1.3
mngal dang nye bar ldan pa nyid kyi sngon rol tu|de ni gnyid song glang po'i dbang po dkar po zhig|rang nyid la ni rab tu zhugs sogs mthong gyur la|de yi mtshan ma nyam thag pa yang thob ma yin BCt_1.4
lha dang rab tu mtshungs pa de yi lha mo de|mngal gyis rigs kyi dpal ni rab tu 'dren byed cing|sgyu ma ngal ba dang ni mya ngan sgyu med par|gtsang la nyon mongs med pa'i dgon par blo gros mdzad BCt_1.5
de ni lum bi zhes bya'i nags mthar gyur pa'i sa|sna tshogs ljon shing sna tshogs shing rta mngon dga' bar|bsam gtan la bzod dben pa'i nags kyi mtha' bzhed ma|'gro ba'i ched dang gnas phyir mi skyong la zhus so BCt_1.6
de yi chos dang ldan la 'phags pa'i zhe 'dod dag|rnam par shes nas ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste|zhi ba'i grong nas sa yi bdag po gshegs gyur te|de yi dga' ba'i rgyu yin rnam par rgyu phyir min BCt_1.7
dpal dang ldan pa'i nags der rgyal po'i bdag ldan ma|rab tu bltams pa'i dus ni yang dag mngon gzigs shing|bla re nye bar phul ba'i gzims mal rab thob ste|mi mo stong phrag dag gis mngon par dga' bar byed BCt_1.8
de nas skar ma rgyal rab ldan par gyur pa'i tshe|brtul zhugs legs par 'dus byas lha mo de yi ni|rtsib logs dag nas 'jig rten phan phyir sras bltams te|tshor ba dang ni bral zhing nad dang bral ba nyid BCt_1.9
ji ltar brla skyes brla nas rgya chen lag pa nas|dbang po dang mtshungs nga la nu ni spyi bo nas|mchan ldan nyid kyang lag pa'i cha shas gsang ba nas|rnam pa de ltar de yi skye ba byung bar gyur BCt_1.10
mngal nas mngon par nges par byung ba gzugs mdzes te|nam mkha' dag las 'phos 'dra skye gnas las ma skyes|bskal pa gcig min rnams su bsgoms pa'i bdag nyid ni|gang zhig yang dag rab tu shes na skyes gyur blun po min BCt_1.11
nyi ma gzhon nu sa la mngon par babs pa bzhin|gsal ba dang ni brtan pas gang zhig mdzes pa ste|de ltar shin tu gsal yang nges par rtog pa na|ri bong gi mtshan ji ltar mig dag phrogs par gyur BCt_1.12
de ni rang gi lus kyi 'od rab 'bar ba yis|sgron ma'i 'od kyang gsal bar byed pa ltar bcom ste|rin thang chen po 'dzam bu chu gser mdzes pa'i mdog|phyogs rnams thams cad rnam par snang zhing gsal bar mdzad BCt_1.13
'khrugs pa ma yin yon po'i skyon dag rab bsal zhing|shin tu brtan pa dang ldan rnam par yangs pa'i 'gros|de ltar mi g.yo rab tu brtan pa'i gom pa bdun|drang srong skar ma bdun dang rab mnyam gshegs par gyur BCt_1.14
byang chub phyir dang 'gro la phan pa'i phyir skyes shing|'di ni bdag gi srid pa'i skye ba tha ma zhes|seng ge'i 'gros 'dra phyogs bzhi dag tu rnam gzigs nas|snod ldan rnams kyi don byed ngag kyang smras par gyur BCt_1.15
nam mkha' dag las rab babs zla ba'i 'od zer dkar|grang dang dro ba'i chu rgyun rnam pa gnyis kyi shugs|lus la yang dag reg pas bde ba bskyed pa'i phyir|mdzes shing yid 'od de yi spyi bor babs par gyur BCt_1.16
dpal ldan bla re bres par gser gyis 'bar zhing mtshan|bai ḍū rya yi rkang pa'i gzims mal la gzims pa|de la gus phyir gser gyi padma'i phyag mnga' ba'i|gnod sbyin bdag rnams kun nas yongs su bskor nas gnas BCt_1.17
mi mngon gyur pa'i lha rnams kyis kyang nam mkha' la|gang gi mthu las mgo bo yis ni rab btud cing|kun nas gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar rnams bzung ste|byang chub ched du mchog gi bsngags pa dag kyang smras BCt_1.18
'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par mchod byas pa'i|lto 'phye che rnams khyad 'phags chos la sred pa'i phyir|gang la rlung g.yab kyis g.yab gus pa'i mig gzir cing|man dā ra ba'i me tog rnams kyis yang dag 'thor BCt_1.19
de bzhin gshegs pa bltams pa'i yon tan gyis tshim pa'i|gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i rnam dag sems can rnams|sdug bsngal nyid du bying ba'i 'gro la phan pa'i phyir|lha rnams 'dod chags bral ba na yang dga' bar gyur BCt_1.20
gang gi rab tu bltams tshe ri rgyal phur bu nyid|rlung gis bsnun pa'i gru ltar sa gzhi g.yos gyur cing|tsan dan dang bcas u-tpal padma'i snying po yi|char pa dag ni nam mkha'i sprin dang bral las babs BCt_1.21
yid 'ong reg na bde ba'i rlung dag byung gyur te|lha yi na bza' dag ni mngon par 'bebs byed cing|nyi ma de nyid lhag par mngon par gsal ba ste|zhi ba'i 'od zer 'dus ma byas pa'i me 'bar ro BCt_1.22
shar dang byang gi mtshams kyi khang pa'i phyogs gcig na|bsil ba'i chu yi khron pa rang byung gyur pa ste|pho brang btsun mo'i 'khor rnams ya mtshan gyur rnams kyis|gang la bya ba rnams ni stegs bzhin rab tu byas BCt_1.23
chos dang ldan pa'i lha dang 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kyis|de ni lta ba'i don du nags tshal rab gang ste|rmad byung ngo mtshar gyur pa nyid kyi shing las kyang|me tog rnams ni dus ma yin par nges par brul BCt_1.24
'tshe bar byed pa'i sems can rnams kyang de yi tshe|phan tshun dag tu phyin te gnod pa mi byed la|'tsho ba'i 'jig rten dag na nad gang ji snyed pa|de dag rnams kyang 'bad pa med par de tshe bcom BCt_1.25
mkha' 'gro'i bya ni mtho min sgra sgrogs ri dags kyang|chu klung dag ni chu yang zhi bar bab gyur la|phyogs rnams rab snang dge ba'i nam mkha' rab mdzes shing|lha yi rnga rnams mkha' la rab tu grags par gyur BCt_1.26
rgud par gyur la mgon ni nye bar thob nas bzhin|'jig rten dag kyang mchog tu rab zhi thob gyur la|'jig rten rnams kyi thar pa'i bla ma rab bltams tshe|'dod pa'i lha nyid kho na dga' ba med par gyur BCt_1.27
shin tu ngo mtshar sras kyi skye ba mthong gyur nas|mi bdag brtan pa yin yang rnam par 'gyur nas song|rab dga' skyes pa nyid dang yid mi bde skyes te|brtse ba las ni mchi ma rnam pa gnyis byung ngo BCt_1.28
mi ma yin pa'i sras po nyid kyi nus pa dang|ma mi rang bzhin kyang ni stobs chung nyid kyi phyir|grang dang dro ba'i chu dag 'dres pa'i chu klung bzhin|lha mo 'jigs pa dang ni dga' bas gang bar 'gyur BCt_1.29
lhag ma spangs te 'jigs pa nyid ni shes byas nas|yid 'ong 'dod pa'i ched du rtogs pa ma yin pa'i|bud med rgan mo rnams kyis bde legs gyur byas shing|gtsang mar byas te lha rnams dag la phyag 'tshal lo BCt_1.30
de yi mtshan nyid dag kyang shes shing thos gyur nas|spyod dang thos dang tshig la grags thob bram ze rnams|rnam rgyas zhal ni ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste|dga' dang 'jigs par gyur pa'i mi yi lha la smras BCt_1.31
mi dag sa la bu ma gtogs pa'i khyad 'phags pa|gzhan gang cung zad 'dod min zhi ba de yi phyir|khyod kyi sgron ma 'di ni rigs kyi sgron ma ste|khyod nyid dga' bar mdzod cig dga' ston da ltar bgyi BCt_1.32
de phyir brtan pa rnam dpyod med par dgar mdzod dang|rigs ni nges pa nyid du mchog tu 'phel bar 'gyur|'di ni khyod kyi bu zhes skyes par gyur pa ste|'jig rten sdug bsngal dag gis mngon par bcom pa'i mgon BCt_1.33
mchog gyur 'di la mchog gyur gser gyi 'od mnga' zhing|sgron ma'i 'od zer dag gi mtshan rnams gang gyur pas|de nyid rtogs par gyur pa'i thub par 'gyur ba 'am|yang na mi bdag sa steng 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur BCt_1.34
sa yi bdag po nyid la gal te dga' 'gyur na|stobs dang chos dag gis ni de'i tshe sa steng du|rgyal po kun gyi thog tu 'di ni gnas 'gyur te|skar ma'i 'od rnams la ni nyi ma'i 'od bzhin no BCt_1.35
de ni gal te thar bzhed nags su gshegs gyur na|mkhyen dang de nyid kyis ni de tshe sa steng du|lugs kun zil gyis mnan nas 'di ni gnas 'gyur te|mtho ba kun la ri rab ri yi rgyal po bzhin BCt_1.36
ji ltar lcags rnams la ni gser dag mchog yin la|ri rnams la ni ri rab chu bo rnams la mtsho|gza' rnams la ni zla ba dud byed rnams la nyi|de ltar khyod kyi sras ni rkang gnyis rnams kyi mchog BCt_1.37
gang gi spyan dag mi 'dzum mi gzir rnam par spangs pa ste|brtan zhing shin tu ring la dkar min rdzi ma dang|gzi brjid ldan pa yin yang 'on kyang zhi ba nyid|'di ni kun nas gzigs pa'i spyan mnga' ci la min BCt_1.38
de nas gnyis skyes rnams la mi bdag gis smra pa|bdag nyid chen po mi skyong snga mas ma mthong ba|mthong zhes khyad 'di gang yin 'di la rgyu mtshan ci|de nas bram ze rnams kyis de nyid la smras pa BCt_1.39
blo dang thos pa las dang grags pa rnams la ni|mi skyong sngon dang phyi ma nyid ni tshad ma min|dngos po'i lugs la 'dir ni bya ba rgyu yin la|'dir yang bdag gi dper brjod dag ni mkhyen par mdzod BCt_1.40
gang zhig rgyal po'i bstan bcos shes ldan ngan spong dag|rigs byed drang srong de gnyis kyis ni ma byas pa|de dag gi sras zhi ba pa wa sangs dang ni|phur bu yis ni dus kyis de nyid bskyed par gyur BCt_1.41
nyams gyur snga ma rnams kyis ma mthong rig byed gang|dbyangs can ma yi bu yis kyang ni slar smras pa|nus med gnas 'jog gis ni ma byas gyur pa gang|rgyas pa yis ni de ltar rnam pa mang por brjod BCt_1.42
'pho byed drang srong chen pos ma bsdebs gyur pa gang|tshig gi rkang pa grog mkhar gyis ni dang por bskyed|gso ba gang yang rgyun shes kyis ni ma mthong ba|phyi nas de ni drang srong rgyun shes bu yis byas BCt_1.43
gang yang gnyis skyes nyid ni ku shas ma rnyed pa|de ni gting dpogs bu yis rgyal po la thob bo|bu ram shing pas dang por ma bsdams gyur pa gang|rgya mtsho la ni dug bcas kyis kyang mtshams bzung ngo BCt_1.44
slob dpon nyid du bram ze'i rnal 'byor cho ga la|gzhan rnams kyis ma thob pa skyed byed gshegs par gyur|khyab 'jug gi ni grags pa'i las rnams gang yin pa|mi rnams la ni dpa' bo la sogs stobs med gyur BCt_1.45
de phyir lang tsho dang ni rigs dag tshad ma yin|la la la lar mchog nyid nyer thob 'jig rten na|rgyal dang drang srong rnams kyi snga mas ma byas pa|de dang de dag rnams ni bu rnams dag gis byas BCt_1.46
de ltar gnyis skyes de rnams kyis ni yid ches te|mi skyong dbugs 'byin dang yang mngon par dga' gyur la|mi 'dod the tshom dag ni yid las rnam bsal te|rab tu dga' ba nyid la lhag par 'dzegs par gyur BCt_1.47
dga' ba yis ni gnyis skyes dam pa de rnams la|bkur sti sngon du 'gro ba'i nor rnams rab phul te|ji skad smras bzhin 'di ni sa yi bdag por gyur|rgas pa thob nas nags rnams su ni 'gro bar shog BCt_1.48
de nas mtshan ma rnams dang dka' thub stobs las ni|skye ba mthar mdzad bltams pa de ni rtogs gyur nas|dam pa'i chos la gus pa'i shākya'i dbang phyug gi|gnas su dkar min drang srong chen po gshegs par gyur BCt_1.49
tshangs pa'i dpal nyid kyis dang dka' thub dpal gyis ni|'bar ba'i tshangs rig rnams kyi tshangs rig de la ni|rgyal po'i bla mas gus pa dang ni bkur sti'i phyir|mi dbang pho brang du ni rab tu spyan drangs so BCt_1.50
de ni sa bdag btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nye logs su|gzhon nu bltams pa la ni dga' ba'i shugs kyis 'ongs|dka' thub mchog las dang ni rgas pa la brten nas|brtan pa nags kyi 'du shes kyis ltar rnam par zhugs BCt_1.51
de nas thub pa gdan la gnas pa de la mi skyong gis|zhabs bsil mchod yon sngon 'gro yang dag rab mchod nas|sngon tshe gnas mchog la ni mtha' can lhas bzhin des|ji ltar nye bar spyod la snyan gsan phab pa'o BCt_1.52
bdag gi rigs ni rjes su bzung phyir nor ldan des|gang zhig bdag la gzigs phyir bcom ldan nyer gshegs la|bka' drin gnang bar mdzod cig zhi ba ci bgyi bgyi|kho bo slob ma lags so thugs rjes mdzad par rigs BCt_1.53
de ltar mi skyong gis ni dngos po thams cad kyis|nye bar gsol btab gyur pa'i thub pa ji lta bzhin|rab rgyas yangs pa'i spyan ni ya mtshan dang bcas pas|zab pa dang ni brtan pa'i tshig rnams smras pa'o BCt_1.54
chos 'dod gtong ba dang ldan 'gron la sdug cing phangs|bdag nyid chen po khyed la 'thad pa 'di yin la|sems dpa' rjes 'gro ye shes lang tsho rjes mthun pa|khyod kyi blo gros gnyen gang de ltar bdag la yin BCt_1.55
de dang de ni gang gis mi skyong drang srong des|phra mo'i chos kyi nor rnams rab tu thob byas nas|rtag par cho ga bzhin du mchod sbyin byas gyur pa|dka' thub rnams kyis phyug cing nor rnams dag gis dbul BCt_1.56
bdag gi nye bar 'ongs la dgos pa gang yin pa|bdag gi de ni gson mdzod dga' bar nyer song khyed|byang chub rtogs pa'i ched du khyod kyi sras bltams zhes|lha yi ngag dag bdag gis nyi ma'i lam du thos BCt_1.57
ngag de thos nas dang ni yid la bsgoms nas dang|mtshan ma rnams kyis shes nas de nas nye bar 'ongs|brgya byin gyi ni rgyal mtshan yang dag bsgrengs pa bzhin|shākya'i rigs kyi rgyal mtshan blta bar 'dod pa yis BCt_1.58
zhes pa'i tshig 'di de ltar thos par gyur nas ni|mi dbang rab tu dga' bas kun nas g.yos gyur te|yum gyi pang du son las gzhon nu blangs nas ni|dka' thub nor can la ni yang dag bstan par gyur BCt_1.59
de nas drang srong che des zhabs la 'khor los mtshan|phyag dang zhabs kyi sor mo dra bas 'brel ba dang|glang po bzhin du mdoms nub smin ma mdzod spur bcas|ya mtshan dang bcas rgyal po'i sras ni mthong bar gyur BCt_1.60
lha mo'i pang na zhugs pa me yi bu bzhin du|ma ma'i pang na zhugs pa mngon par mthong nas ni|byung gyur rdzi ma'i mtha' ru mchi ma rnam byung ste|dbugs med gyur nas gyen du lta la zhal phyogs gyur BCt_1.61
mig dag mchi mas yongs gang dkar min mthong nas ni|bu la brtse ba'i phyir ni mi skyong 'dar gyur te|mchi ma dang ni gre ba kha zhing ldab ldib bcas|thal mo sbyar zhing yan lag btud de dris par gyur BCt_1.62
gang gi lus ni lha las bar na cung zad cig|gang gi skye ba ngo mtshar mang po'i sgron ma ste|gang gi don ni mchog tu 'gyur bar smra ba ste|rab tu mthong nas brtan pa gang phyir mchi ma 'ong BCt_1.63
bcom ldan gzhon nu brtan pa'i tshe can yin snyam mam|bdag gi mya ngan ched du skyes pa min nam ci|bdag la chu yi snyim pa ci zhig ltar rnyed de|'di ni dus kyis 'thung phyir nye bar 'ongs ma yin BCt_1.64
bdag gi snyan grags gter ni mi zad yin snyam mam|nges par bdag gi rigs kyi lag nor yin snyam ci|nges par pha rol tu ni rab tu 'gro snyam mam|gnyid par gyur kyang bu ni phye ba'i mig gcig yod BCt_1.65
bdag gi rigs kyi myu gu skyes pa ma rgyas par|yongs su skams pa'i skal ba can zhig min snyam mam|khyab bdag myur bar gsungs shig bdag la zhi ba med|gnyen 'dun rnams kyi bu la brtse ba khyed kyis rig BCt_1.66
de ltar mi 'dod blo yis 'khrul ba byung gyur pa|rig nas mi dbang rgyal la thub pa des smras pa|bdag gis smras pa gang de the tshom med pa de|mi skyong khyed kyi blo gros gzhan gang ma gyur cig BCt_1.67
'di yi gzhan gyur mtshon min bdag gi rnam 'gyur te|'on kyang rang la slu bar rab mtshon rnam par 'khrugs|skye ba zad pa'i rnyed par sla min rtogs pa po|'di skyes bdag gi 'gro ba la ni dus yin no BCt_1.68
rgyal srid rnam par spangs nas yul rnams la mi gnas|'bad pa drag po rnams kyis de nyid thob byas nas|'di ni 'gro la gti mug mun pa rnam 'joms phyir|ye shes rang bzhin nyi ma rab tu 'bar bar 'gyur BCt_1.69
sdug bsngal rgya mtsho nad rnam bkram pa'i dbu ba can|rga ba'i dba' rlabs 'chi ba'i shugs ni drag po las|'gro ba nyam thag bying bar gyur rnams 'di yis ni|ye shes gru bo chen po yis ni sgrol bar byed BCt_1.70
shes rab chu yi shugs la brtan pa'i tshul khrims ngogs|ting nge 'dzin ni bsil ba'i brtul zhugs ngang pa 'phyo|'di yi mchog gi chos kyi chu bo rab bskor la|sred pas nyam thag gson pa'i 'jig rten 'thung bar byed BCt_1.71
sdug bsngal gyis nyam thag dang yul gyis bsgribs rnams dang|'khor ba'i 'brog dgon 'jigs par gnas pa rnams la ni|lam rab chud zos rnams la lam 'gro rnams bzhin du|'dis ni rnam par dag pa'i lam dag 'chad par 'gyur BCt_1.72
yul gyi bung shing can gyi 'dod chags me yis ni|'jig rten skye bo rnam par bsregs par gyur ba la|sos ka'i tha mar sprin chen gyis ni char bzhin du|'di yis chos kyi char gyis rab tu sim byed 'gyur BCt_1.73
sred pa'i sgo gtan ma rig mun pa'i sgo glegs can|sgo la skye dgu rnams kyi 'thon pa'i rgyu las ni|'di yis mchog rab kun nas rnyed par dka' ba yi|dam pa'i chos kyi sgras ni rnam par 'byed par 'gyur BCt_1.74
rang gi las kyi zhags pa rnams kyis yongs dkris shing|sdug bsngal dag gis mngon par zil non rten med pa'i|'jig rten rnams kyi rdzogs pa'i byang chub brnyes nas kyang|chos kyi rgyal po 'dis ni 'ching ba thar mdzad 'gyur BCt_1.75
rmongs sam 'dod pa'i bde ba yis sam rgyags las rung|'di yi mthar thug chos gang thos par mi byed pa|mi yi 'jig rten 'dir de mya ngan bya ba'i gnas|de phyir khyed nyid 'di la mya ngan ma byed cig BCt_1.76
yon tan rgya mtsho 'di las 'khrul gyur bdag gi ni|bsam gtan rnams ni thob kyang don byas med nyid de|de yi dam chos ma thos pa las kho bo ni|mtho ris dag na gnas kyang phun tshogs med pa snyam BCt_1.77
de ltar don thos bshes dang bcas shing btsun mor bcas|yid mi bde ba dor nas mi dbang dgar gyur la|rnam pa de ltar bdag gi bu ni 'di'o zhes|des ni bdag nyid la ni snying po ldan par bsams BCt_1.78
'phags pa'i chos rnams kyis kyang 'gro bar 'gyur ro zhes|bsam pa'i rnam par gzung bya snying la byas gyur te|nges par 'di ni mi sdug chos kyi phyogs min la|rigs rgyud nyams pa las ni 'on kyang 'jigs pa mthong BCt_1.79
de nas bu la rnam par 'khrugs pa'i rgyal po la|bu yi nges pa'i de nyid rig par byas nas su|gus bcas gyen du gzugs mthong dkar min thub pa ni|rlung gi lam gyis ji ltar 'ongs par gshegs par gyur BCt_1.80
blo gros byas pa'i sring mo'i bu yang mthong nas ni|thub pa'i gsung mnyan pa dang de yi lugs la ni|rnam mang rjes su brtse ba yis ni legs pa des|sdug pa'i bu bzhin du ni sbyor ba byed du bcug BCt_1.81
sras po skyes pas tshim pa'i mi yi bdag po yang|yul la song ba'i 'ching ba rnams ni rnam spangs te|sras kyi yid 'ong sras po bltams pa'i las dag ni|rigs dang 'dra bar ji lta ba bzhin byed du bcug BCt_1.82
zhag bcu yongs su 'das par gyur pa nyid kyi tshe|mchog gi dga' ba rab ldan snyoms par gyur pa'i yid|sras las mchog tu 'gyur phyir lha yi mchod pa ni|bzlas brjod dang ni sbyin sreg bkra shis la sogs byas BCt_1.83
gzhan yang brgya dang stong phrag yongs su gang ba'i grangs|brtan dang stobs ldan bu rnams gser gyu rwar bcas shing|rgas pa nye bar 'ongs min 'o ma ldan pa'i ba|rang gi sras 'phel phyir na gnyis skyes rnams la byin BCt_1.84
de nas snyoms pa'i bdag nyid kyis ni rnam mang yul|rang sems tshim par byed pa'i bya ba rnams byas nas|yon tan ldan zhing dge ba'i yud tsam nges pa na|grong khyer rab tu 'jug la dga' bas blo gros mdzad BCt_1.85
de nas mche gnyis mche ba las byung rin thang che|dkar po dkar po'i me tog gis spras nor bu'i sgron|khri la dge ba'i phyir ni lha mo sras ldan ma|lha rnams la ni rab tu btud nas bsnyen par gyur BCt_1.86
de nas gnas brtan skye mo rjes 'brang sras mgon ma|bdag po ldan ma grong la mdun du rab zhugs nas|mchod ldan lha na lha rnams kyis ni brgya byin bzhin|mi bdag nyid kyang grong pa'i tshogs kyis gshegs par gyur BCt_1.87
de nas gdong drug skyes pas yid ches dbang phyug bzhin|shākya'i rgyal pos grong khyer rnam par khyab mdzad de|zhal ni dga' bas rab gang 'di dang 'di zhes pa'i|srid 'phel rgyas pa dang ni grags dang snyan pa mdzad BCt_1.88
de nas mi yi bdag po'i sras bltams cher skyes pas|ser skya zhes pa'i grong khyer ljongs dang bcas pa de|gnod sbyin grong ni phun tshogs 'dod pa skyes pa na|lha yi bu mo rnams kyis bkram bzhin dga' bar gyur BCt_1.89
| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | gzhon nu sku bltams pa'i le'u ste dang po'o ||
skye dang rga ba mthar song bdag skyes bdag pham de'i|skyes pa nas brtsams mi nyin nyi mas rgyal po de|chu yi shugs rnams kyis ni chu bo sin dhu bzhin|nor dang glang po rta dang bshes rnams 'phel bar gyur BCt_2.1
nor rnams dang ni rin po che dang bzang po'i gser|de dang de ni byas dang ma byas pa nyid kyang|yid la re ba yi rang bzhin du khur gyur pa|de la gcig tu phan pa'i cha shas gter rnyed gyur BCt_2.2
gang zhig padma dang mtshungs gnyis 'thung rnams kyis kyang|dkyil 'khor 'di la nye bar 'ong bar mi nus pa'i|gangs dang ldan pa'i glang chen chang gis dregs de rnams|'bad pa las kyang gzhan du de la nye bar gnas BCt_2.3
sna tshogs mtshan mas mtshan zhing gsar ba'i gser sga dang|de bzhin gzhan rnams dag gis brgyan byas rngog ma 'phyang|stobs dang byams pa dang ni nor gyis thob pa yi|'di yi mgyogs 'gro rnams kyis grong khyer phye mar byas BCt_2.4
de bzhin 'di yi yul 'khor du ni tshim dang rgyas|legs ma rdul ldan yon tan ldan pa'o mar ldan|rab mchog be'u rnams dang bcas pa'i ba rnams ni|'o ma mang po 'jo ba mang po byung bar gyur BCt_2.5
'di yi dgra bo dbus gnas nyid du song gyur pa|dbus gnas gyur pa mdza' bshes nyid du rab tu song|khyad par du ni bshes gnyen brtan por song ba ste|'di yi phyogs dag gnyis te dgra yang yod ma yin BCt_2.6
de bzhin du ni 'di yi 'jam rlung 'brug gi sgra|glog gi 'phreng ba 'khyil ba yis ni brgyan pa'i sprin|rdo char dang ni thog lhung nyes pa rnams kyis gzhan|yul du dus la lha yis char pa phab par gyur BCt_2.7
zhing gi las kyi ngal dub byed pa nyung ngus kyang|'bru ni 'bras bu ldan pa dus sbyor bzhin skyes te|de rnams nyid kyang 'di yi sman du byung gyur la|bcud dang snying po yis kyang mngon par lhag pa nyid BCt_2.8
g.yul du rab tu zhugs la kun tu 'joms pa bzhin|lus la the tshom za bar byed pa'i dus na yang|rab bzhin gnas shing bde ba nyid du nad med par|dus kyi dbang gis mi mo rnams ni rab tu btsas BCt_2.9
brtul zhugs ldan rnams ma gtogs nor rdzas dman na yang|mi rnams pha rol rnams las don du gnyer mi byed|mngon par don du gnyer la 'phags pa nor 'phra yang|de tshe 'ga' zhig dag ni rgyab kyis phyogs ma gyur BCt_2.10
de tshe rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la ni 'ga'|gnyen la zhe sa med min mi ster ba yang med|brtul zhugs med pa nyid min rdzun med 'tshe med pa|sgra mi bsgrags kyi sras po lta bu byung bar gyur BCt_2.11
der yang skyed mos tshal dang lha gnas dka' thub gnas|khron pa rdzing dang dge bcu 'du ba'i gnas rnams kyi|bya ba rnams ni mtho ris bzhin du nyer thob nas|chos 'dod rnams kyis mngon sum du ni rab tu mdzad BCt_2.12
mu ge dang ni 'jigs dang nad rnams las grol zhing|dgar gyur skye bo mtho ris bzhin du mngon par dga'|bdag pos bdag mo la 'am mo yis bdag por rung|phan tshun log par mngon par spyod pa dag kyang med BCt_2.13
dga' ba'i ched du 'dod la 'ga' zhig gis ma bsnyen|'dod pa'i don du nor ni 'ga' zhig gis ma bsrungs|nor gyi don du chos la 'ga' zhig gis ma spyad|chos kyi ched du tshe ba 'ga' zhig gis ma byas BCt_2.14
rkun po sogs dang dgra yang nyams par rang gnas te|pha rol mya ngan med pa ji lta ba nyid bzhin|rang gi 'khor lo pha rol 'khor lo las grol te|rgyal po de la bde dang lo legs byung bar gyur BCt_2.15
de yi tshe na rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la|de skyes pa na nyi ma'i sras po'i yid shes bzhin|dga' bar spyad par gyur la sdig pa rab nyams shing|chos rnams 'bar zhing nyon mongs rnams ni zhi bar gyur BCt_2.16
gang phyir rnam pa de ltar don kun grub pa dang|rgyal po'i rigs kyi phun sum tshogs pa byung gyur te|de phyir mi skyong gis ni sras po de yi mtshan|don kun grub pa zhes bya 'di ni rab tu mdzad BCt_2.17
lha mo sgyu ma yang ni lha yi drang srong mtshungs|bu yi nus mthu rnam par spangs pa mthong nas ni|bltams la rab tu dga' mas bzod par ma nus te|de nas gnas pa'i phyir du lhar ni gshegs par gyur BCt_2.18
de nas lha yi mngal dang mtshungs pa'i gzhon nu la|byams pa'i rang bzhin gyis kyang khyad par med pa yi|ma yi nu mo mdangs mnyam pa yi rang bzhin la|yang dag skyed bcug bdag las skyes pa lta bur gyur BCt_2.19
de nas nyi ma gzhon nu 'char rir gnas 'dra dang|rlung gis rab tu bud par gyur pa'i me bzhin dang|skar ma'i bdag po mun min phyogs la gnas pa ltar|gzhon nu de ni rim gyis yang dag 'phel bar gyur BCt_2.20
de nas ring thang chen po'i tsan dan rnams dang ni|rin chen 'phreng ba sman gyi snying por bcas rnams dang|ri dags rab tu sbyar ba'i gser gyi shing rta dang|'di yi ched du bshes kyi khyim rnams dag nas blangs BCt_2.21
lang tshe nyid dang rjes su mthun pa'i rgyan rnams dang|gser gyi rang bzhin ri dags glang chen rta rnams dang|gser dang dngul gyis bris pa'i mi chung gzugs rnams dang|shing rta ba glang byung dus yang dag sbyar rnams blangs BCt_2.22
de ni lang tsho rjes mthun yul la nye spyod pa|de rnams kyis ni yul la nyer spyad la|dpal dang brtan pa yis dang blo dang dpal gyis kyang|byis pa yin yang byis min rab mtshungs byung bar gyur BCt_2.23
lang tsho gzhon nu shin tu 'das nas yang dag par|'du byed las ni rab tu thob nas dus su ni|lo mang dag gis rtogs bya nyin zhag nyung ngu yis|rang dang rjes su mthun pa'i rig pa rnams ni blangs BCt_2.24
drang srong chen po dkar min las ni sngon rol du|de yi nye legs don gyi skal ba thos nas ni|nags su gshegs par 'gyur zhes shākya'i rgyal po yis|'dod pa rnams la chags pa bskyed du bcug par gyur BCt_2.25
brtan pa'i tshul khrims spyod pa spyan gyi rigs de las|ngo tsha dang ni dul ba nyer ldan legs ldan ma|grags 'dzin ma zhes grags pa rnam par yangs pa ma|btsun mor mngon par brjod pa'i dpal mo 'di la blangs BCt_2.26
kun byed gzhon nu dang ni rab tu mtshungs pa yi|mchog gi lus kyis snang zhing gsal ba de nyid ni|shākya'i rgyal po'i mna' ma de dang thabs gcig tu|bde sogs ma dang mig stong ldan bzhin mngon par dga' BCt_2.27
yid kyang skyod par byed la cung zhig rab log pa|gang gis mthong mi 'gyur zhes rjes su bsams byas nas|sa la rab tu spyod min lding khang lto nyid du|gnas dag mi skyong gis ni de la rnam par bstan BCt_2.28
de nas gzhal med nam mkhar sa la spyod pa bzhin|ston ka'i dus kyi chu ster sprin ni dkar po yi|dus sbyor kun tu bde ba'i gzhi yi lding khang la|bud med rnams kyi sil snyan rgya chen rnams kyis rnam par gshegs BCt_2.29
gser gyis bsdams pa'i rnga shing can gyi rdza rnga'i skad|mi mo'i lag pa'i rtse mos mngon par brdungs pa yi|lha mchog ma yi gar dang mnyam pa'i gar rnams kyis|ti se'i gangs ltar de yi pho brang mdzes par gyur BCt_2.30
ngag dang bzo dang rol dang rnam 'gyur rnams kyis kyang|rgyags dang rtse dang rgod pa dngar mo rnams kyis dang|smin ma bskyod pa yis dang phyed mig lta rnams kyis|de la der ni mi mo rnams ni dga' bar gyur BCt_2.31
de nas de ni 'dod pa rten par mkhas pa yis|dga' bas dregs pa'i bud med rnams kyis bzung gyur la|gzhal med khang gi rgyab nas bsod nams las can bzhin|gzhal med khang gi rgyab nas sa la ma gshegs so BCt_2.32
mi skyong gis kyang de nyid bskyed pa'i ched las ni|de yi 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i don gyis bskul gyur te|sdig pa las ni dga' bral zhi la mngon dga' zhing|legs la skal bar bgos shing dul la bsnyen par gyur BCt_2.33
brtan min bzhin du 'dod pa'i bde la ma zhen la|ma rungs bskyed ma la ni yang dag chags ma gyur|brtan pas dbang po'i rta ni stabs las rnam thul zhing|gzhen dang grong khyer pa rnams yon tan rnams kyis rgyal BCt_2.34
gzhan gyi sdug bsngal phir ni rig pa ma brjod la|ye shes dge ba gang yang de la lhag par brjod|des ni rang gi skye dgu rnams la ji lta bar|de ltar skye dgu rnams la dge ba'i bsngags pa mdzad BCt_2.35
skar ma rgyal snang shes ldan sras po lhag pa'i lha|ji lta bar ni de yi tshe ring phyir mchod de|chung min me la bsreg bya rnams ni bsregs gyur la|gnyis skyes rnams la gser dang ba lang rnams kyang byin BCt_2.36
'gram stegs chab rnams kyis dang yon tan chab rnams kyis|gtsang sbra'i ched du lus dang yid la khrus byas te|rig byed du ni nye bar bstan pa'i chang rnams dang|zhi ba bdag skyes snying la zhi ba'i bde la 'thungs BCt_2.37
gang zhig don dang mi ldan zhi ba ma smras la|gang zhig dga' ba dang bral de nyid ma brjod de|zhi ba de nyid med dang rtsub pa'i de nyid phyir|ngo tsha ba yis bdag nyid kho na brjod ma nus BCt_2.38
don ldan 'dod pa rnams dang mi 'dod pa rnams la|chags pa'i skyon la brten nas rab tu 'thob min te|dge ba'i tha snyad gtsang ma la ni bsnyen gyur la|mchod sbyin la yang ma mos de ltar ji lta bzhin BCt_2.39
sred pa dang ldan mngon par 'ongs la de ma thag|sbyin bya chu 'dra rnams kyis skom pa bcad gyur la|g.yul las ma gtogs ye shes kyi ni sta ri yis|dgra bo rnams kyi nga rgyal chen po bcom par gyur BCt_2.40
bcig ni rnam par dul la des ni bdun bsrungs shing|bdun po nyid ni dor la lnga po dag ni bsrungs|sde tshan gsum po thob la sde tshan gsum rtogs shing|sde tshan gnyis po shes la sde tshan gnyis po spangs BCt_2.41
nyes pa byas kyang rab tu bskyabs nas gzhom bya la|'tshe bar mi byed khro bas kyang ni gzigs ma yin|de rnams dag la 'bras bu zhi bas bcings gyur la|de rnams dag ni 'dor ba tshul ma yin phyir mthong BCt_2.42
drang srong rnams kyi mchog gi brtul zhugs spyad gyur la|yun ring yang dag bzung ba'i sha 'khon zhugs rnams dor|yon tan dri ldan snyan dag rnams ni thob gyur la|dri ma can du byed pa'i rdul rnams rnam par dor BCt_2.43
rab tu mi gnas gtor ma'i dpya ni ma blangs la|pha rol dngos po rnams la mngon par rlom ma byas|dgra rnams la ni chos ma yin pa ma smras la|khro bo rnams ni snying gis bzung ba ma yin no BCt_2.44
zhi ba'i bdag nyid sems ni rnam par rab dad la|rnal 'byor rab tu ldan pa'i dbang po rnams ci ltar|der ni de ltar sa bdag rab tu sgyur ba can|'bangs dang grong khyer pa rnams de lta nyid du byas BCt_2.45
de nas mdzes ma'i 'o ma 'dzin pa dang ldan ma|grags 'dzin ma ni rang gi grags pa 'dzin ma la|zas gtsang sras po'i sras po sgra gcan dgra yi zhal|sgra gcan 'dzin zhes bya ba dus su skyes par gyur BCt_2.46
de nas 'dod pa'i bu mnga' mchog gis yid ches te|rigs brgyud 'phel ba rab mtshon sa skyong rgyal po ni|ji lta nyid du sras po rab tu skyes la dga'|de lta nyid du sras po'i sras po skyes la dga' BCt_2.47
bdag gi bu yi bur gyur pa la brtse ba ni|bdag bzhin gang las yin zhes dga' ba skyes gyur te|dus su des ni cha ga de dang de dmigs shing|bu la dga' ba mtho ris bzhin du 'dzegs par gyur BCt_2.48
rgyal po'i khyu mchog grags dang snyan pas mtshan rnams kyi|dang po'i bskal ba rnams kyi lam la gnas nas ni|dkar po ma dor dka' thub rnams la dka' thub dang|'tshe ba dor ba'i mchod sbyin rnams kyis mchod par gyur BCt_2.49
rgyal po'i dpal gyis dang ni dka' thub dpal gyis kyang|bsod nams las can de ni de nas 'bar gyur la|rigs dang blo dang mdzad spyod kyis kyang gsal ba ste|gzi brjid stong gi 'od zer bzhin du rab tu 'phro BCt_2.50
rang byung las byung mchod byed sngags ni mchod byas nas|sras gnas ched du brtan pa'i dpal gyis bzlas byas shing|dka' thub byed pa'i las rnams byas gyur skye dgu rnams|skyed 'dod skye dgu'i bdag bzhin dang po'i dus su'o BCt_2.51
mtshon cha spangs shing bstan bcos rnam par shes gyur la|nye bar zhi la bsnyen zhing nges la rnam par bzod|dbang ldan bzhin du yul rnams gang la ma bsnyen la|yab mes bzhin du yul rnams kun la gzigs par gyur BCt_2.52
des kyang bu yi ched du rgyal srid bzung gyur la|bu ni rigs kyi don du rigs ni grags pa'i phyir|grags pa mtho ris ched du mtho ris bdag nyid phyir|chos kyi don du bdag nyid gnas la 'dod par gyur BCt_2.53
de ltar des ni dam pa rnams kyis nges thob pa'i|thos pa las grub chos ni rnam pa sna tshogs byas|gang las bdag gi bus ni bu yi ngo mthong nas|nags tshal nyid du 'gro mi 'gyur zhes mgon bslangs so BCt_2.54
bdag la yang dag gnas pa'i dpal ni bsrung 'dod pa'i|sa skyong rnams kyis sa la bu ni bsrung ba ste|chos ni 'dod pa'i mi yi dbang po de yis kyang|yul rnams 'dor ba med par bu ni chos las bsrungs BCt_2.55
byang chub sems dpa' yul la bde ba'i ro shes thams cad kyang|srags bskyed pa na dpe med sems dpa' nags su gshegs gyur te|de phyir nye bar bsags pa'i las ni rtsa nas bskyed pa'i phyir|de ni zhi ba ma thob de srid dga' ba bsnyen par gyur BCt_2.56

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | btsun mo'i 'khor na gnas pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o ||
de nas re zhig dus nas 'jam po'i rtswa rnams dang|khu byug pho ni gyen du skad 'don rkang 'thung rnams|glu rnams dang ni nges ldan skyed mos tshal rnams ni|padma'i 'byung gnas kyis brgyan des ni thos par gyur BCt_3.1
de nas bud med skye bo rnams ni dga' ba yi|grong khyer skyed mos tshal gyi yid 'ong dngos thos te|khyim gi nang du mngon par bkag pa'i klu bzhin du|phyi rol rab tu 'gro ba'i ched du blo mdzad do BCt_3.2
de nas sras su mngon brjod yid 'ong de yi ni|dgongs pa mi skyong gis ni nges par thos gyur nas|brtse ba'i phun sum tshogs pas lang tshor 'ongs pa ru|ltad mo dag la rnam par gshegs par bka' stsal to BCt_3.3
gzhon nu shin tu gzhon nu'i sems dang ldan pa ni|yang dag skyo ba'i sems su ma gyur zhes sems shing|nyam thag tha dad skye bo kun nas 'dus pa ni|rgyal po'i lam du phyir la rnam par bzlog pa ste BCt_3.4
nying lag dman pa rnams dang dbang po ma tshang rnams|'khogs pa nad pa la sogs bkren rnams phyogs rnams su|de nas mchog tu zhi bas yang dag rab bton nas|rgyal po'i lam rnams dag ni mchog tu mdzes par byas BCt_3.5
de nas dpal ldan rgyal po'i lam ni byas pa na|dpal ldan rnam par dul ba rjes 'brang gzhon nu ni|gzhal yas khang pa'i logs nas dus su mngon babs nas|mngon par rjes gnang byas pa mi skyong la mngon gshegs BCt_3.6
de nas mi dbang bu la mchi ma byung gyur te|mgo la nye bar bsnoms te yun ring rnam gzigs nas|song zhig ces ni tshig gi bka' dag bstsal gyur la|brtse ba dag las de ni yid kyis ma btang ngo BCt_3.7
de nas de ni 'dzam bu chu gser sga 'dzin pa'i|legs par bslabs pa'i mgyogs 'gro ba'i yis sbyar ba yi|dbang po ma nyams mkhas shing gcang la 'od zer 'chang|gser gyi rang bzhin shing rta la ni yang dag 'dzegs BCt_3.8
de nas 'bras spos me tog 'bar ba rab bkram zhing|phreng ba rnam dpyangs rab tu g.yo ba'i ba dan can|zla ba skar ma dang bcas bar snang la bzhin du|'brang ba rjes 'brang lam ni rab tu thob par gyur BCt_3.9
ya mtshan gyur las rab tu rgyas pa'i mig rnams ni|u-tpal sngon po'i phyed 'dra rnams kyis bkram pa ni|rgyal po'i lam la dal bu dal bus gshegs gyur te|grong khyer skye bo rnams kyis kun nas mngon par dga' BCt_3.10
kha cig de la zhi ba'i yon tan gyis bstod la|de bzhin gzhan rnams gsal ba nyid kyis phyag 'tshal zhing|kha cig dag ni 'di la mngon du phyogs nas kyang|dpal dang tshe yi rnam par rgyas la shis pa brjod BCt_3.11
zhar ba sgur po nang pa mi'u thung rnams kyi|tshogs pa rnams ni rigs chen rnams las nges bral nas|mi mo rnams ni nges par zhugs gnas phra rnams las|lha yi rjes 'gro rgyal mtshan bzhin du rab tu btud BCt_3.12
de nas gzhon nu nges par gshegs shes gtam dag ni|bsgo bya skye las bud med rnams kyis thos gyur nas|bkur 'os skye bos mngon par rjes gnang byas pa rnams|blta bar 'dod pas lding khang shong du song bar gyur BCt_3.13
yon tan ska rags brul zhing gegs byas de rnams ni|gnyid log rab tu sad pas lta byed 'khrugs pa rnams|gnas lugs gtam gyis rnam par brgyan rnams rnam bzhag ste|ya mtshan gyur pas dogs med par ni yongs su song BCt_3.14
gzhal yas khang gi skad kyi 'og gi sgra rnams dang|dril chung sgra rnams dang ni gdu bu'i sgra rnams kyis|rnam par skrag gyur khyim gyi bya ba'i tshogs rnams ni|phan tshun shugs rnams las kyang yang dag kun nas gtor BCt_3.15
gang zhig 'dir ni yan lag rab mchog ma rnams ni|myur ba rab tu skyes gyur tsam tsom skyes rnams kyi|'o ma 'dzin rnams rgyas shing skyed smad shing rta ni|yangs pa rnams kyis lci ba nyid phyir 'gro ba bzung BCt_3.16
mtha' gcig legs par rab tu sbyar ba'i rgyan rnams ni|rnam par sbas pa rnam par gsal bas ngo tsha bas|skyen por 'gro ba nus pa yin yang gzhan mo yis|'gro ba nges par bzung ste myur min song bar gyur BCt_3.17
phan tshun rab tu bcer bas ril por gyur pa rnams|yang dag drud las bskyod gyur rna lung 'khyil ba can|de dag rnams kyi de tshe sgra bcas rgyan rnams ni|rlung bgrod skar khung rnams su rab tu zhi bar gyur BCt_3.18
rlung bgrod skar khung rnams las rnam par 'thon pa rnams|phan tshun thang chod gyur pa'i lung rna 'khyil ba rnams|bud med rnams kyi 'dam skyes 'dra ba'i 'dam skyes zhal|lding khang rnams su bkod pa rnams ni rnam par mdzes BCt_3.19
de nas khang bzangs lang tsho ma rnams kyis khyab cing|ya mtshan las ni rab phye skar khung rnams kyis ni|lha mo dang bcas gzhal med rnams kyis nam mkha' bzhin|dpal dang ldan pa'i grong khyer kun nas mdzes par gyur BCt_3.20
skar khung rnams kyi rnam par spangs pa ma yin las|phan tshun 'gram par bkod pa'i rna lung can rnams kyi|'dam skyes padma rnams kyi tshogs rnams bcings pa bzhin|rab myos mchog ma rnams kyi zhal ni mdzes par gyur BCt_3.21
gzhon nu de la lam du rnam par lta ba yi|bud med de rnams sa la 'gro 'dod ltar mdzes shing|gyen du gdong phyogs de la rab tu blta ba yi|mi rnams gnam la 'gro bar 'dod bzhin mdzes par gyur BCt_3.22
lus dang dpal gyis mchog tu 'bar bar gyur pa yi|rgyal po'i sras de mthong nas bud med de rnams ni|nges par dgongs par gzhan min bsam pa dag pa yis|'di yi chung ma skal ba bzang zhes dal bus smras BCt_3.23
gzugs kyis dngos su me tog tog can dang mtshungs shing|rnam par ring zhing rgyas pa'i dpung pa can 'di ni|dpal nyid dor nas chos la nye bar gshegs shes te|de la de dag rnams kyis zhe sa kho na byas BCt_3.24
rnam par dul la gtsang zhing brtan pa'i cha lugs can|grong pa rnams kyis de ltar rgyal po'i lam khyab pa|de ni sngon du gzhon nus mthong nas dga' ba ste|bdag gi srid pa gzhan ma cung zhig brtags pa 'dra BCt_3.25
grong khyer de yang mtho ris bzhin du rab dga' ba|mngon par gzigs nas gtsang mar gnas pa'i lha rnams kyis|sa gzhi skyong ba'i sras po yang dag bskul don du|'khogs pa'i mi rgan rab tu 'gro bar sprul gyur to BCt_3.26
de nas gzhon nu yis ni rga bas zil non zhing|mi rnams las ni tha dad dbyibs can de gzigs nas|g.yo ba mang cing de nyid du ni zhugs pa'i spyan|chags par gyur cing kha lo 'dzin pa la smras so BCt_3.27
mngon par nyer 'ong mi de su yin 'dren pa kye|skra rnams dkar zhing dbyug pa la ni lag pas brten|smin mas kun nas mig g.yogs 'khogs shing yan lag dud|rnam 'gyur 'di ni tha mal gang 'dod yin nam ci BCt_3.28
de skad ces smras shing rta rab tu 'dren pa po|lha mchog de rnams nyid kyis blo ni rmongs byas shing|don ni bsrung bya yin yang skyon med mthong gyur te|de yis sa skyong bdag nyid skyes la nges par gsol BCt_3.29
gzugs kyi gnod byed stobs kyi rnam par za ba po|dga' ba rnams kyi 'joms byed mya ngan rnams kyi sa|dran pa rnams kyi nyams byed dbang po rnams kyi dgra|'di ni rgas pa zhes bya gang gis 'di bcom mo BCt_3.30
'dis kyang byis pa nyid na 'o ma 'thungs gyur cing|dus kyis sa la yongs su gnyid log gyur pa ste|rim gyis lus rab ldan pa'i lang tsho gyur nas kyang|rim gyis de nyid kho na rga bar nye bar song BCt_3.31
de skad ces smras rgyal po'i bdag nyid skyes pa de|cung zhig 'dar zhing kha lo sgyur la 'di skad smras|skyon 'di kho bo la yang 'byung ba yin 'am ci|de bzhin 'di la kha lo sgyur ba yis gsol to BCt_3.32

de ltar song na 'dren pa rta rnams phyir bzlog la|khyod ni khyim nyid du ni skyen par rab tu song|rgas pa'i 'jigs pa'i sems su gnas pa kho bo la|skyed mos tshal gyi sa la bde ba ga la yod BCt_3.37

gang gi tshe na der yang bde ba ma rnyed de|rgas pa rgas pa zhes ni rab tu yongs su rtogs|de nas mi dbang gis ni rjes gnang de ni slar|rim gyis de nyid kho nas phyi rol gshegs par gyur BCt_3.39

de nas kha lo sgyur bas smras pa zhi ba kye|'di yi 'khams ni rab 'khrugs rab stobs rab tu 'phel|nad ces bya ba mngon brjod shin tu don med chen po ste|nus kyang gang gis de ni rang dbang med par byas BCt_3.42
rjes su brtse bcas mi ni de la gzigs bzhin du|rgyal po'i sras des slar yang 'di skad ces smras pa|skyes gyur skyon de so sor 'di nyid kho na'i 'am|nad kyi 'jigs pa skye dgu rnams kyi spyi la yin BCt_3.43
de nas shing rta rab tu 'dren pa des smras pa|gzhon nu nyes pa de ni thun mong gyur pa ste|de ltar nad rnams dag gis yongs su bcer ba ni|nad mthar phyin na 'jig rten dga' bar nye bar gshegs BCt_3.44
de ltar don thos sems ni khong du chud pa de|chu rlabs nang song ri bong can bzhin rab 'dar zhing|brtse ba thugs rje mnga' bas gsung ngag tshig 'di ni|cung zhig dngar ba'i dbyangs kyis rab tu smras pa'o BCt_3.45

'di ni nges par skye dgu rnams kyi mthar thug ste|'jig rten pa dag 'jigs pa spangs shing bag med la|mi rnams dag gi sems rnams sra ba snyam pa ste|lam la gnas rnams de ltar rang bzhin nyid du gnas BCt_3.61
de phyir 'dren pa shing rta'i kha ni phyir bzlog dang|bdag cag sa la rnam par rgyu ba'i yul dus min|nyam thag dus su rnam par nyams pa shes nas ni|sems dang bcas pa gang 'dra 'di na bag med yin BCt_3.62

de nas me tog rgyas ldan gzhon nu'i rkang 'thung zhing|yongs su skor zhing rab dka' mos pa'i khu byug can|gzhal med khang ldan padma dang bcas mdzes pa'i rdzing|dga' ba'i tshal 'dra dge ba'i nags de gzigs par gyur BCt_3.64

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | bsngags ldan phyir la bzlog pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o ||

song nas de na kau shām rgyal po'i kha ba dang ni|gtsug lag khang gi sa la so sor yang dag rgyas|dpal ldan mnyam zhing mdzes la yid 'ongs shing ldan pa|der ni de yis rgyal byed kyi ni tshal mthong ngo BCt_18.82

de nas thub pa sna tshogs tha dad blo can gyi|ston pas thams cad ye shes kyis ni zil mnan nas|bcu phyed phrag ri nas dang grong khyer nas rim gyis|rgyal po bum pas bsnyen pa'i grong khyer du gshegs so BCt_19.1
de nas slob ma stong phrag tsam ni dul ba na|gshegs so des ni yab kyi yul ni rab tu thob|de nas de la rjes su 'dzin pa mdzad bzhed pa|rang gi grong gyi gnas la mtha' ru bsnyen pa'o BCt_19.2

de nas de ni 'ongs pa thos nas sa skyong ni|dga' ba yongs ldan sems kyis blta bar 'dod pa yis|grong khyer ba ni kun gyis rjes su 'gro byas pa|myur bas brtan pa spangs shi ng bsu ba la gshegs so BCt_19.4

| sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | rgyal byed kyi tshal rab tu bzhes pa'i le'u ste nyi shu pa'o ||

de phyir mun par 'dod pa 'di ni spongs 'dod pa|chang ni spangs la rang bzhin 'du shes thob par gyis|'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i 'dam ni rgyas par chags pa ste|slar yang de ltar gnyis 'thung dbang po ma ltung cig BCt_21.57

de nas drang srong chen po'i thugs kyi ting nge 'dzin|rnam pa de ltar rnal 'byor stobs las mdzad pa nyid|sku tshe ji ltar gyur pa sngon du btang ba ste|rdzu 'phrul mthu las mtshungs pa med pa 'tsho bar gyur BCt_23.70
des ni sku tshe btang ba'i yud tsam de la ni|bud med myos ma bzhin du sa ni g.yos gyur la|ma yis tshos pa'i lhun po'i rdo ba rim bzhin du|phyogs rnams dag las sgron ma chen po rnams lhung ngo BCt_23.71
de bzhin kun nas dbang po'i rdo rje mi bzad rnams|glog dang bcas shing mi yi snying po can g.yos shing|bskal pa 'jig che 'jig rten bsreg par 'dod pa bzhin|phyogs rnams thams cad rnams su me dag 'bar bar gyur BCt_23.72
shing rnams kyis ni phung po 'gogs pa rnams por zhing|ri rnams kyis ni rtsi mo rnams ni dor ba ste|rlung gis mngon par gang ba'i rdo ba'i phug bzhin du|mkha' la rnga rnams kyi ni ma rungs sgra rnams bsgrags BCt_23.73
de nas de ltar kun tu bskyod tshe yud tsam la|mi yi 'jig rten na dang lha dang nam mkha' la|ting nge 'dzin chen po las rnam par bzhengs mdzad nas|thub pa chen pos gsung ni 'di nyid gsungs pa'o BCt_23.74
shing rta srog shing rnam par jams pa dang 'dra ba'i|tshe btang lus po nang gi stobs las 'dren bgyi zhing|sgo nga'i skye gnas pa rnams sgo nga phye nas bzhin|srid pa'i 'ching las tshe dang lhan cig 'grol bar bgyi BCt_23.75

sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las | sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o || ||
